 1
 On the day of Pooja, first of all, put red or yellow cloth on a big and clean outpost and place the idols of lakshmi-ganesh on it

 2
 All the worshipers should sit in front of the idols
 3
 Now place a kalash on the rice near Lakshmiji

 3
 yah kalash varun kaa pratik hota he

 ek deepak chaowkee ke dayee ore rakhen or doosraa murtiyon ke charnon main

 4

 6

 Progress from Milk to CD4 Counts He said that the effect of goat milk on AIDS patients for a total of nine months was studied and it was found that there was a significant progress in CD4 Counts in the initial month in goat milk patients
 unki sankhya badhane lagi jo aids ke marijon kii pratirohak kshamta banaae rakhane ke liye jaruri hoti he

 bhuvi ne 82 ran dekar chah wicket liye lekin usase pehle 1936 main amar singh ne 35 ran dekar chah wicket liye the
 Bhubaneswar achieved this feat in his eighth Test match at Lord's called the Mecca of Cricket
 stokes ke baad stuart broad kaa wicket chatka bhuvi ne bharat ke liye pehali pari main chah wicket hasil kiye
 Bhubaneswar is the third bowler from Uttar Pradesh to take five wickets at Lord's
 bhuvi se pehle aar
 P
 singh ne 2007 main or praveen kumaar ne 2011 main paanch wicket jhatakane kii uplabdhi hasil kii thi
 Lords is a tradition of the Maidan
 yahaan shatak lagane vaale yaa phir pari main paanch yaa usase adhik wicket lene vaale khilaadi kaa naam onors board par darj kiya jaataa he
